## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x1CD3 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x4EB3)
  1: 0x1CD6 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Restore default settings
  2: 0x1CD8 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x46AD)
  3: 0x1CDB [0x21] END_EVENT
  4: 0x1CDC [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

SUBROUTINE_46AD:
  5: 0x46AD [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdi1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
  6: 0x46BE [0x55] WAIT_LOAD_SCHEDULER: Wait for scheduler "fdi1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=200*
  7: 0x46CD [0x1B] RETURN

SUBROUTINE_46CE:
  8: 0x46CE [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
  9: 0x46DF [0x55] WAIT_LOAD_SCHEDULER: Wait for scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=200*
 10: 0x46EE [0x1B] RETURN

SUBROUTINE_4EB3:
 11: 0x4EB3 [0x5D] SET_MUSIC_VOLUME(volume=0*, fade_time=180*)
 12: 0x4EB8 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x46CE)
```
